    function insertNewsletter(name, email1, address, city, dob, doa, gender) {


        var name = $("#name").val();
        var textPattern = /^[a-zA-Z ]*$/;
        var ret = textPattern.test(name);

        var email1 = $("#email1").val();
        var atpos = email1.indexOf("@");
        var dotpos = email1.lastIndexOf(".");

        var address = $("#address").val();

        var city = $("#city").val();
        var textPattern2 = /^[a-zA-Z ]*$/;
        var ret2 = textPattern2.test(city);
        var ret2 = textPattern2.test(city);


        var dob = $("#dob").val();
        var doa = $("#doa").val();
        var gender = $("#gender").val();




        if (name == "") {
            str = 1;
            $("#name-error").show();
            $("#name").focus();

        }

        else if (!ret) {
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").show();
            $("#name").focus();


        }

        else if (atpos < 1 || dotpos < atpos + 2 || dotpos + 2 >= email.length) {
            str += 1;
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").hide();
            $("#email-error").show();
            $("#email").focus();

        }


        else if (address == "") {
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").hide();
            $("#email-error").hide();
            $("#address-error").show();
            $("#address").focus();

        }

        else if (city == "") {
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").hide();
            $("#email-error").hide();
            $("#address-error").hide();
            $("#city-error").show();
            $("#city").focus();

        }

        else if (!ret2) {
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").hide();
            $("#email-error").hide();
            $("#address-error").hide();
            $("#citychars-error").show();
            $("#city").focus();

        }

        else if (dob == "") {
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").hide();
            $("#email-error").hide();
            $("#address-error").hide();
            $("#city-error").hide();
            $("#dob-error").show();
            $("#dob").focus();

        }

        else if (gender == "") {
            $("#name-error").hide();
            $("#namechars-error").hide();
            $("#email-error").hide();
            $("#address-error").hide();
            $("#city-error").hide();
            $("#dob-error").hide();
            $("#gender-error").show();
            $("#gender").focus();

        }
        else {
            //alert("hi");

            $.post("ajax/addNewsletterInfo.php", {"name": name, "email1": email1, "address": address, "city": city, "dob": dob, "doa": doa, "gender": gender}, function (data) {
                if (data == 'YES') {
                    //alert(data);
                    $('#join').hide();
                    $('.form_tp').html("Thank you for registering.");

                }
            });

        }
        return false;
    }
